name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:2 Reviews
rating:3
posted:Posted April 26, 2024
msg:Medium review.
Let me start with the main point. Friends who need to order takeout can forget about this hotel!
Because the hotel does not have a food delivery robot, and it does not require the deliveryman to go upstairs. You need to wait for the elevator from the thirty-odd floors of a maze-like building A or building B in the hotel to go down to the takeout cabinet on the first floor to pick up the food, and this will directly cause your deliveryman to put the food down and leave, and it is reasonable not to notify you.
Second, friends who like quietness can forget about this hotel. Because this hotel is more like an office building in Buildings A and B. There are many people and it is noisy, and you have to wait for ten minutes for each elevator.
I have never seen a hotel that can undertake five or six ** activities on the same day (there are pictures and the truth), and there are all kinds of idle people, from uncles in basketball uniforms, noisy white-collar workers, to pheasants waiting for guests downstairs.
Third, breakfast became the last straw that broke the camel's back. The number of people for breakfast obviously exceeded the carrying limit. I waited for more than ten minutes to go up and down the elevator, and it was full of people. The eggs for breakfast are always empty, without any additions. There is never any coffee either.
If the hotel is committed to the money of the conference partners, it is unfair to Ctrip users who pursue consumption experience.
Fourthly, the good part is that the hotel room facilities are relatively good, with a bathtub, refrigerator, and they are all clean.
But if you book this hotel for more than 324 yuan, then congratulations to Hefei Fengda Hotel!

msg:I chose this hotel when I came to Hefei to watch a concert. I stayed for two nights. The location is quite convenient. It is a 20-minute drive from Hefei South Station. There is a Haidilao milk tea shop downstairs and a commercial plaza not far away. It was perfect when I first arrived at the hotel, but the toiletries drawer was wet... When I looked for the sewing kit, I found that it was still used by the previous person and not replaced... There was only half a roll of toilet paper. When I asked the room aunt to deliver it the next morning, the aunt wanted to clean it immediately, but it was inconvenient to refuse. The aunt also said that there was a wedding banquet in the afternoon and there was no time to clean... It seemed like it was our fault... After watching the concert on the second night, I arrived at the hotel at 11:30. When I got to the door, the room card could not be opened. I called the front desk from the staircase phone but no one answered. I went downstairs to scan the room card. The room card for two nights was given only one night's permission. I was really angry. I hope the hotel will strengthen employee training.
